  Fontconfig configuration is done via /etc/fonts/conf.avail and conf.d.
  Read /etc/fonts/conf.d/README for more information.

  Configuration via /etc/fonts/local.conf is still possible,

  Main systemwide configuration should be done by symlinks

  cd /etc/fonts/conf.d

  dir=/tmp/totem/pkg/totem/usr/share/locale/$lang/LC_MESSAGES; \
  /bin/sh /tmp/totem/src/totem-3.18.1/build-aux/install-sh -d $dir; \
  if test -r $lang.gmo; then \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 $lang.gmo $dir/totem.mo; \
    echo "installing $lang.gmo as $dir/totem.mo"; \
  else \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 ./$lang.gmo $dir/totem.mo; \
    echo "installing ./$lang.gmo as" \
	 "$dir/totem.mo"; \
  fi; \
  if test -r $lang.gmo.m; then \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 $lang.gmo.m $dir/totem.mo.m; \
    echo "installing $lang.gmo.m as $dir/totem.mo.m"; \
  else \
    if test -r ./$lang.gmo.m ; then \
      /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 ./$lang.gmo.m \
	$dir/totem.mo.m; \
      echo "installing ./$lang.gmo.m as" \
	   "$dir/totem.mo.m"; \
    else \
      true; \
    fi; \
  fi; \
done
